<div  class="block block-views block-views-slide-block ">
	<div class="width content">
 	 
  	 	   	
 	 
 	 

        
  
  
  
      <div  id="flexslider-1" class="flexslider optionset-default">
  <ul class="slides"><li>  
  <div class="views-field views-field-title">        <span class="field-content">
  <img typeof="foaf:Image" src="https://www.brown.edu/academics/archaeology/sites/academics-archaeology/files/styles/slide/public/surachi-nuraghe-2014_0.jpg?itok=eblQPa1i" width="861" height="573" alt="" /> 
<div class="overlay">
<h2>Archaeology at Brown University</h2>

  <div class="field-body">
    <p>
	The Joukowsky Institute for Archaeology and the Ancient World promotes the investigation, understanding, and enjoyment of the archaeology and art of the ancient Mediterranean, Egypt, and the Near East.  We work in close collaboration with our colleagues in Brown University's Department of Anthropology whose research is focused on the study of the material remains of the ancient, historic, and modern Americas.
</p>
  </div>
 
</div>
</span>  </div></li>
<li>  
  <div class="views-field views-field-title">        <span class="field-content">
  <img typeof="foaf:Image" src="https://www.brown.edu/academics/archaeology/sites/academics-archaeology/files/styles/slide/public/OtherSideofRome-2016c.jpg?itok=YIFFseue" width="861" height="573" alt="" /> 
<div class="overlay">
<h2>An Interdisciplinary Community</h2>

  <div class="field-body">
    <p>
	The goal of the Institute is to foster an interdisciplinary community of interest in the archaeology of the ancient world, and in the discipline of archaeology more generally.
</p>
  </div>
 
</div>
</span>  </div></li>
<li>  
  <div class="views-field views-field-title">        <span class="field-content">
  <img typeof="foaf:Image" src="https://www.brown.edu/academics/archaeology/sites/academics-archaeology/files/styles/slide/public/styles/slide/public/SLAM2017-KRMR.jpg?itok=8lyic9Hd" width="861" height="573" alt="" /> 
<div class="overlay">
<h2>Our Mandate</h2>

  <div class="field-body">
    <p>
	Our mandate is to promote research, fieldwork, teaching, and public outreach, with the Institute’s associated faculty, students, staff, and facilities serving as a hub for this activity.
</p>
  </div>
 
</div>
</span>  </div></li>
</ul></div>

          <li class="views-row"><div  about="/academics/archaeology/news/2017/09/new-website-new-year" typeof="sioc:Item foaf:Document" class="ds-1col node-article node-teaser view-mode-teaser clearfix">

  
  
  <div class="field-image">
    <a href="/academics/archaeology/news/2017/09/new-website-new-year"><img typeof="foaf:Image" src="https://www.brown.edu/academics/archaeology/sites/academics-archaeology/files/styles/medium/public/Convocation2016b.jpg?itok=I-BU5bF4" width="220" height="146" alt="" /></a>  </div>
<div class="list-chunk-220">
                <h2><a href="/academics/archaeology/news/2017/09/new-website-new-year">A New Website for a New Year</a></h2>        

  <div class="field-start-end-date">
    <time  property="dc:date" datatype="xsd:dateTime" content="2017-09-06T00:00:00-04:00" datetime="2017-09-06T00:00:00-04:00">Wednesday September 6, 2017</time>  </div>
</div></div>

</li>
      </ul></div>

<div  class="block block-views block-views-fieldwork-featured-project ">
	<div class="width content">
 	 
  	 	   	  <h2 class="title">Featured Project</h2>
 	   	
 	 
 	 

        
  
  
  
        <div class="views-row">
    <article  class="node-project node-promoted node-teaser " about="/academics/archaeology/content/survey-and-landscape-archaeology-montserrat-west-indies" typeof="sioc:Item foaf:Document" role="article">
  
        <h2><a href="/academics/archaeology/content/survey-and-landscape-archaeology-montserrat-west-indies" rel="bookmark">Survey and Landscape Archaeology on Montserrat, West Indies</a></h2>
    <span property="dc:title" content="Survey and Landscape Archaeology on Montserrat, West Indies" class="rdf-meta element-hidden"></span>
  
  <div class="content">
    
  <div class="field-proj-image">
    <a href="/academics/archaeology/content/survey-and-landscape-archaeology-montserrat-west-indies"><img typeof="foaf:Image" src="https://www.brown.edu/academics/archaeology/sites/academics-archaeology/files/styles/large/public/project/media/Montserrat1.JPG?itok=DmNLA-je" width="480" height="360" alt="" /></a>  </div>

  <div class="field-body">
    <p>
	SLAM aims to create a thorough inventory of known and unknown archaeological sites in the northern non-exclusion zone of Montserrat in the West Indies, home to numerous significant prehistoric and historic archaeological remains now under severe threat from volcanic activity and resulting population relocation.
</p>
  </div>
  </div>

  
  </article>

  </div>

  
  
  
  
      <div class="view-footer">
      <div class="view-all"><a href="research-projects/brown-university-fieldwork" class="view-all">View All</a></div>
    </div>
  
  

 	 	</div>
</div>

<div  class="block block-views block-views-slide-block ">
	<div class="width content">
 	 
  	 	   	
 	 
 	 

        
  
  
  
      <div  id="flexslider-1" class="flexslider optionset-default">
  <ul class="slides"><li>  
  <div class="views-field views-field-title">        <span class="field-content">
  <img typeof="foaf:Image" src="https://www.brown.edu/academics/archaeology/sites/academics-archaeology/files/styles/slide/public/surachi-nuraghe-2014_0.jpg?itok=eblQPa1i" width="861" height="573" alt="" /> 
<div class="overlay">
<h2>Archaeology at Brown University</h2>

  <div class="field-body">
    <p>
	The Joukowsky Institute for Archaeology and the Ancient World promotes the investigation, understanding, and enjoyment of the archaeology and art of the ancient Mediterranean, Egypt, and the Near East.  We work in close collaboration with our colleagues in Brown University's Department of Anthropology whose research is focused on the study of the material remains of the ancient, historic, and modern Americas.
</p>
  </div>
 
</div>
</span>  </div></li>
<li>  
  <div class="views-field views-field-title">        <span class="field-content">
  <img typeof="foaf:Image" src="https://www.brown.edu/academics/archaeology/sites/academics-archaeology/files/styles/slide/public/OtherSideofRome-2016c.jpg?itok=YIFFseue" width="861" height="573" alt="" /> 
<div class="overlay">
<h2>An Interdisciplinary Community</h2>

  <div class="field-body">
    <p>
	The goal of the Institute is to foster an interdisciplinary community of interest in the archaeology of the ancient world, and in the discipline of archaeology more generally.
</p>
  </div>
 
</div>
</span>  </div></li>
<li>  
  <div class="views-field views-field-title">        <span class="field-content">
  <img typeof="foaf:Image" src="https://www.brown.edu/academics/archaeology/sites/academics-archaeology/files/styles/slide/public/styles/slide/public/SLAM2017-KRMR.jpg?itok=8lyic9Hd" width="861" height="573" alt="" /> 
<div class="overlay">
<h2>Our Mandate</h2>

  <div class="field-body">
    <p>
	Our mandate is to promote research, fieldwork, teaching, and public outreach, with the Institute’s associated faculty, students, staff, and facilities serving as a hub for this activity.
</p>
  </div>
 
</div>
</span>  </div></li>
</ul></div>

<div  class="block block-views block-views-fieldwork-featured-project ">
	<div class="width content">
 	 
  	 	   	  <h2 class="title">Featured Project</h2>
 	   	
 	 
 	 

        
  
  
  
        <div class="views-row">
    <article  class="node-project node-promoted node-teaser " about="/academics/archaeology/content/survey-and-landscape-archaeology-montserrat-west-indies" typeof="sioc:Item foaf:Document" role="article">
  
        <h2><a href="/academics/archaeology/content/survey-and-landscape-archaeology-montserrat-west-indies" rel="bookmark">Survey and Landscape Archaeology on Montserrat, West Indies</a></h2>
    <span property="dc:title" content="Survey and Landscape Archaeology on Montserrat, West Indies" class="rdf-meta element-hidden"></span>
  
  <div class="content">
    
  <div class="field-proj-image">
    <a href="/academics/archaeology/content/survey-and-landscape-archaeology-montserrat-west-indies"><img typeof="foaf:Image" src="https://www.brown.edu/academics/archaeology/sites/academics-archaeology/files/styles/large/public/project/media/Montserrat1.JPG?itok=DmNLA-je" width="480" height="360" alt="" /></a>  </div>

  <div class="field-body">
    <p>
	SLAM aims to create a thorough inventory of known and unknown archaeological sites in the northern non-exclusion zone of Montserrat in the West Indies, home to numerous significant prehistoric and historic archaeological remains now under severe threat from volcanic activity and resulting population relocation.
</p>
  </div>
  </div>

  
  </article>

  </div>

  
  
  
  
      <div class="view-footer">
      <div class="view-all"><a href="research-projects/brown-university-fieldwork" class="view-all">View All</a></div>
    </div>

<div  class="block block-views block-views-events-block-1 ">
	<div class="width content">
 	 
  	 	   	  <h2 class="title">Events</h2>
 	   	
 	 
 	 

        
  
  
  
        <div class="views-row">
    <article  class="node-event node-promoted node-teaser " about="/academics/archaeology/content/anthony-tuck-umass-amherst-palace-politics-evolution-elite-domestic-architecture-poggio" typeof="sioc:Item foaf:Document" role="article">
  
        <h2><a href="/academics/archaeology/content/anthony-tuck-umass-amherst-palace-politics-evolution-elite-domestic-architecture-poggio" rel="bookmark">Anthony Tuck (UMass at Amherst) - Palace Politics: The Evolution of Elite Domestic Architecture at Poggio Civitate</a></h2>
    <span property="dc:title" content="Anthony Tuck (UMass at Amherst) - Palace Politics: The Evolution of Elite Domestic Architecture at Poggio Civitate" class="rdf-meta element-hidden"></span>
  
  <div class="content">
    
  <div class="field-start-end-date">
    <time  property="dc:date" datatype="xsd:dateTime" content="2017-10-17T00:00:00-04:00" datetime="2017-10-17T00:00:00-04:00">Tuesday, October 17, 2017</time>  </div>

  <div class="field-start-end-time">

<div  class="block block-views block-views-slide-block ">
	<div class="width content">
 	 
  	 	   	
 	 
 	 

        
  
  
  
      <div  id="flexslider-1" class="flexslider optionset-default">
  <ul class="slides"><li>  
  <div class="views-field views-field-title">        <span class="field-content">
  <img typeof="foaf:Image" src="https://www.brown.edu/academics/archaeology/sites/academics-archaeology/files/styles/slide/public/surachi-nuraghe-2014_0.jpg?itok=eblQPa1i" width="861" height="573" alt="" /> 
<div class="overlay">
<h2>Archaeology at Brown University</h2>

  <div class="field-body">
    <p>
	The Joukowsky Institute for Archaeology and the Ancient World promotes the investigation, understanding, and enjoyment of the archaeology and art of the ancient Mediterranean, Egypt, and the Near East.  We work in close collaboration with our colleagues in Brown University's Department of Anthropology whose research is focused on the study of the material remains of the ancient, historic, and modern Americas.
</p>
  </div>
 
</div>
</span>  </div></li>
<li>  
  <div class="views-field views-field-title">        <span class="field-content">
  <img typeof="foaf:Image" src="https://www.brown.edu/academics/archaeology/sites/academics-archaeology/files/styles/slide/public/OtherSideofRome-2016c.jpg?itok=YIFFseue" width="861" height="573" alt="" /> 
<div class="overlay">
<h2>An Interdisciplinary Community</h2>

  <div class="field-body">
    <p>
	The goal of the Institute is to foster an interdisciplinary community of interest in the archaeology of the ancient world, and in the discipline of archaeology more generally.
</p>
  </div>
 
</div>
</span>  </div></li>
<li>  
  <div class="views-field views-field-title">        <span class="field-content">
  <img typeof="foaf:Image" src="https://www.brown.edu/academics/archaeology/sites/academics-archaeology/files/styles/slide/public/styles/slide/public/SLAM2017-KRMR.jpg?itok=8lyic9Hd" width="861" height="573" alt="" /> 
<div class="overlay">
<h2>Our Mandate</h2>

  <div class="field-body">
    <p>
	Our mandate is to promote research, fieldwork, teaching, and public outreach, with the Institute’s associated faculty, students, staff, and facilities serving as a hub for this activity.
</p>
  </div>
 
</div>
</span>  </div></li>
</ul></div>

</div>

<div  class="block block-views block-views-fieldwork-featured-project ">
	<div class="width content">
 	 
  	 	   	  <h2 class="title">Featured Project</h2>
 	   	
 	 
 	 

        
  
  
  
        <div class="views-row">
    <article  class="node-project node-promoted node-teaser " about="/academics/archaeology/content/survey-and-landscape-archaeology-montserrat-west-indies" typeof="sioc:Item foaf:Document" role="article">
  
        <h2><a href="/academics/archaeology/content/survey-and-landscape-archaeology-montserrat-west-indies" rel="bookmark">Survey and Landscape Archaeology on Montserrat, West Indies</a></h2>
    <span property="dc:title" content="Survey and Landscape Archaeology on Montserrat, West Indies" class="rdf-meta element-hidden"></span>
  
  <div class="content">
    
  <div class="field-proj-image">
    <a href="/academics/archaeology/content/survey-and-landscape-archaeology-montserrat-west-indies"><img typeof="foaf:Image" src="https://www.brown.edu/academics/archaeology/sites/academics-archaeology/files/styles/large/public/project/media/Montserrat1.JPG?itok=DmNLA-je" width="480" height="360" alt="" /></a>  </div>

  <div class="field-body">
    <p>
	SLAM aims to create a thorough inventory of known and unknown archaeological sites in the northern non-exclusion zone of Montserrat in the West Indies, home to numerous significant prehistoric and historic archaeological remains now under severe threat from volcanic activity and resulting population relocation.
</p>
  </div>
  </div>

  
  </article>

  </div>

        <h2><a href="/academics/archaeology/content/brown-bag-series-archaeology-nicholas-laluk-anthropology" rel="bookmark">Brown Bag Series in Archaeology: Nicholas Laluk (Anthropology)</a></h2>
    <span property="dc:title" content="Brown Bag Series in Archaeology: Nicholas Laluk (Anthropology)" class="rdf-meta element-hidden"></span>
  
  <div class="content">
    
  <div class="field-start-end-date">
    <time  property="dc:date" datatype="xsd:dateTime" content="2017-10-26T00:00:00-04:00" datetime="2017-10-26T00:00:00-04:00">Thursday, October 26, 2017</time>  </div>

  <div class="field-start-end-time">

          <div class="above-content">
            
    
<div  class="block block-views block-views-slide-block ">
	<div class="width content">
 	 
  	 	   	
 	 
 	 

        
  
  
  
      <div  id="flexslider-1" class="flexslider optionset-default">
  <ul class="slides"><li>  
  <div class="views-field views-field-title">        <span class="field-content">
  <img typeof="foaf:Image" src="https://www.brown.edu/academics/archaeology/sites/academics-archaeology/files/styles/slide/public/surachi-nuraghe-2014_0.jpg?itok=eblQPa1i" width="861" height="573" alt="" /> 
<div class="overlay">
<h2>Archaeology at Brown University</h2>

  <div class="field-body">
    <p>
	The Joukowsky Institute for Archaeology and the Ancient World promotes the investigation, understanding, and enjoyment of the archaeology and art of the ancient Mediterranean, Egypt, and the Near East.  We work in close collaboration with our colleagues in Brown University's Department of Anthropology whose research is focused on the study of the material remains of the ancient, historic, and modern Americas.
</p>
  </div>
 
</div>
</span>  </div></li>
<li>  
  <div class="views-field views-field-title">        <span class="field-content">
  <img typeof="foaf:Image" src="https://www.brown.edu/academics/archaeology/sites/academics-archaeology/files/styles/slide/public/OtherSideofRome-2016c.jpg?itok=YIFFseue" width="861" height="573" alt="" /> 
<div class="overlay">
<h2>An Interdisciplinary Community</h2>

  <div class="field-body">
    <p>
	The goal of the Institute is to foster an interdisciplinary community of interest in the archaeology of the ancient world, and in the discipline of archaeology more generally.
</p>
  </div>
 
</div>
</span>  </div></li>
<li>  
  <div class="views-field views-field-title">        <span class="field-content">
  <img typeof="foaf:Image" src="https://www.brown.edu/academics/archaeology/sites/academics-archaeology/files/styles/slide/public/styles/slide/public/SLAM2017-KRMR.jpg?itok=8lyic9Hd" width="861" height="573" alt="" /> 
<div class="overlay">
<h2>Our Mandate</h2>

  <div class="field-body">
    <p>
	Our mandate is to promote research, fieldwork, teaching, and public outreach, with the Institute’s associated faculty, students, staff, and facilities serving as a hub for this activity.
</p>
  </div>
 
</div>
</span>  </div></li>
</ul></div>

</div>

<div  class="block block-views block-views-fieldwork-featured-project ">
	<div class="width content">
 	 
  	 	   	  <h2 class="title">Featured Project</h2>
 	   	
 	 
 	 

        
  
  
  
        <div class="views-row">
    <article  class="node-project node-promoted node-teaser " about="/academics/archaeology/content/survey-and-landscape-archaeology-montserrat-west-indies" typeof="sioc:Item foaf:Document" role="article">
  
        <h2><a href="/academics/archaeology/content/survey-and-landscape-archaeology-montserrat-west-indies" rel="bookmark">Survey and Landscape Archaeology on Montserrat, West Indies</a></h2>
    <span property="dc:title" content="Survey and Landscape Archaeology on Montserrat, West Indies" class="rdf-meta element-hidden"></span>
  
  <div class="content">
    
  <div class="field-proj-image">
    <a href="/academics/archaeology/content/survey-and-landscape-archaeology-montserrat-west-indies"><img typeof="foaf:Image" src="https://www.brown.edu/academics/archaeology/sites/academics-archaeology/files/styles/large/public/project/media/Montserrat1.JPG?itok=DmNLA-je" width="480" height="360" alt="" /></a>  </div>

  <div class="field-body">
    <p>
	SLAM aims to create a thorough inventory of known and unknown archaeological sites in the northern non-exclusion zone of Montserrat in the West Indies, home to numerous significant prehistoric and historic archaeological remains now under severe threat from volcanic activity and resulting population relocation.
</p>
  </div>
  </div>

  
  </article>

  </div>

          </ul>
        </div>

  <main>
    <div class="marginator">
		 
          <div class="above-content">
            
    
<div  class="block block-views block-views-slide-block ">
	<div class="width content">
 	 
  	 	   	
 	 
 	 

        
  
  
  
      <div  id="flexslider-1" class="flexslider optionset-default">
  <ul class="slides"><li>  
  <div class="views-field views-field-title">        <span class="field-content">
  <img typeof="foaf:Image" src="https://www.brown.edu/academics/archaeology/sites/academics-archaeology/files/styles/slide/public/surachi-nuraghe-2014_0.jpg?itok=eblQPa1i" width="861" height="573" alt="" /> 
<div class="overlay">
<h2>Archaeology at Brown University</h2>

  <div class="field-body">
    <p>
	The Joukowsky Institute for Archaeology and the Ancient World promotes the investigation, understanding, and enjoyment of the archaeology and art of the ancient Mediterranean, Egypt, and the Near East.  We work in close collaboration with our colleagues in Brown University's Department of Anthropology whose research is focused on the study of the material remains of the ancient, historic, and modern Americas.
</p>
  </div>
 
</div>
</span>  </div></li>
<li>  
  <div class="views-field views-field-title">        <span class="field-content">
  <img typeof="foaf:Image" src="https://www.brown.edu/academics/archaeology/sites/academics-archaeology/files/styles/slide/public/OtherSideofRome-2016c.jpg?itok=YIFFseue" width="861" height="573" alt="" /> 
<div class="overlay">
<h2>An Interdisciplinary Community</h2>

  <div class="field-body">
    <p>
	The goal of the Institute is to foster an interdisciplinary community of interest in the archaeology of the ancient world, and in the discipline of archaeology more generally.
</p>
  </div>
 
</div>
</span>  </div></li>
<li>  
  <div class="views-field views-field-title">        <span class="field-content">
  <img typeof="foaf:Image" src="https://www.brown.edu/academics/archaeology/sites/academics-archaeology/files/styles/slide/public/styles/slide/public/SLAM2017-KRMR.jpg?itok=8lyic9Hd" width="861" height="573" alt="" /> 
<div class="overlay">
<h2>Our Mandate</h2>

  <div class="field-body">
    <p>
	Our mandate is to promote research, fieldwork, teaching, and public outreach, with the Institute’s associated faculty, students, staff, and facilities serving as a hub for this activity.
</p>
  </div>
 
</div>
</span>  </div></li>
</ul></div>

<div  class="block block-views block-views-fieldwork-featured-project ">
	<div class="width content">
 	 
  	 	   	  <h2 class="title">Featured Project</h2>
 	   	
 	 
 	 

        
  
  
  
        <div class="views-row">
    <article  class="node-project node-promoted node-teaser " about="/academics/archaeology/content/survey-and-landscape-archaeology-montserrat-west-indies" typeof="sioc:Item foaf:Document" role="article">
  
        <h2><a href="/academics/archaeology/content/survey-and-landscape-archaeology-montserrat-west-indies" rel="bookmark">Survey and Landscape Archaeology on Montserrat, West Indies</a></h2>
    <span property="dc:title" content="Survey and Landscape Archaeology on Montserrat, West Indies" class="rdf-meta element-hidden"></span>
  
  <div class="content">
    
  <div class="field-proj-image">
    <a href="/academics/archaeology/content/survey-and-landscape-archaeology-montserrat-west-indies"><img typeof="foaf:Image" src="https://www.brown.edu/academics/archaeology/sites/academics-archaeology/files/styles/large/public/project/media/Montserrat1.JPG?itok=DmNLA-je" width="480" height="360" alt="" /></a>  </div>

  <div class="field-body">
    <p>
	SLAM aims to create a thorough inventory of known and unknown archaeological sites in the northern non-exclusion zone of Montserrat in the West Indies, home to numerous significant prehistoric and historic archaeological remains now under severe threat from volcanic activity and resulting population relocation.
</p>
  </div>
  </div>

  
  </article>

  </div>

  
  
  
  
      <div class="view-footer">
      <div class="view-all"><a href="research-projects/brown-university-fieldwork" class="view-all">View All</a></div>
    </div>

<div  class="block block-views block-views-slide-block ">
	<div class="width content">
 	 
  	 	   	
 	 
 	 

        
  
  
  
      <div  id="flexslider-1" class="flexslider optionset-default">
  <ul class="slides"><li>  
  <div class="views-field views-field-title">        <span class="field-content">
  <img typeof="foaf:Image" src="https://www.brown.edu/academics/archaeology/sites/academics-archaeology/files/styles/slide/public/surachi-nuraghe-2014_0.jpg?itok=eblQPa1i" width="861" height="573" alt="" /> 
<div class="overlay">
<h2>Archaeology at Brown University</h2>

  <div class="field-body">
    <p>
	The Joukowsky Institute for Archaeology and the Ancient World promotes the investigation, understanding, and enjoyment of the archaeology and art of the ancient Mediterranean, Egypt, and the Near East.  We work in close collaboration with our colleagues in Brown University's Department of Anthropology whose research is focused on the study of the material remains of the ancient, historic, and modern Americas.
</p>
  </div>
 
</div>
</span>  </div></li>
<li>  
  <div class="views-field views-field-title">        <span class="field-content">
  <img typeof="foaf:Image" src="https://www.brown.edu/academics/archaeology/sites/academics-archaeology/files/styles/slide/public/OtherSideofRome-2016c.jpg?itok=YIFFseue" width="861" height="573" alt="" /> 
<div class="overlay">
<h2>An Interdisciplinary Community</h2>

  <div class="field-body">
    <p>
	The goal of the Institute is to foster an interdisciplinary community of interest in the archaeology of the ancient world, and in the discipline of archaeology more generally.
</p>
  </div>
 
</div>
</span>  </div></li>
<li>  
  <div class="views-field views-field-title">        <span class="field-content">
  <img typeof="foaf:Image" src="https://www.brown.edu/academics/archaeology/sites/academics-archaeology/files/styles/slide/public/styles/slide/public/SLAM2017-KRMR.jpg?itok=8lyic9Hd" width="861" height="573" alt="" /> 
<div class="overlay">
<h2>Our Mandate</h2>

  <div class="field-body">
    <p>
	Our mandate is to promote research, fieldwork, teaching, and public outreach, with the Institute’s associated faculty, students, staff, and facilities serving as a hub for this activity.
</p>
  </div>
 
</div>
</span>  </div></li>
</ul></div>

<div  class="block block-views block-views-fieldwork-featured-project ">
	<div class="width content">
 	 
  	 	   	  <h2 class="title">Featured Project</h2>
 	   	
 	 
 	 

        
  
  
  
        <div class="views-row">
    <article  class="node-project node-promoted node-teaser " about="/academics/archaeology/content/survey-and-landscape-archaeology-montserrat-west-indies" typeof="sioc:Item foaf:Document" role="article">
  
        <h2><a href="/academics/archaeology/content/survey-and-landscape-archaeology-montserrat-west-indies" rel="bookmark">Survey and Landscape Archaeology on Montserrat, West Indies</a></h2>
    <span property="dc:title" content="Survey and Landscape Archaeology on Montserrat, West Indies" class="rdf-meta element-hidden"></span>
  
  <div class="content">
    
  <div class="field-proj-image">
    <a href="/academics/archaeology/content/survey-and-landscape-archaeology-montserrat-west-indies"><img typeof="foaf:Image" src="https://www.brown.edu/academics/archaeology/sites/academics-archaeology/files/styles/large/public/project/media/Montserrat1.JPG?itok=DmNLA-je" width="480" height="360" alt="" /></a>  </div>

  <div class="field-body">
    <p>
	SLAM aims to create a thorough inventory of known and unknown archaeological sites in the northern non-exclusion zone of Montserrat in the West Indies, home to numerous significant prehistoric and historic archaeological remains now under severe threat from volcanic activity and resulting population relocation.
</p>
  </div>
  </div>

  
  </article>

  </div>

  
  
  
  
      <div class="view-footer">
      <div class="view-all"><a href="research-projects/brown-university-fieldwork" class="view-all">View All</a></div>
    </div>
  
  

 	 	</div>
</div>

<div  class="block block-views block-views-slide-block ">
	<div class="width content">
 	 
  	 	   	
 	 
 	 

        
  
  
  
      <div  id="flexslider-1" class="flexslider optionset-default">
  <ul class="slides"><li>  
  <div class="views-field views-field-title">        <span class="field-content">
  <img typeof="foaf:Image" src="https://www.brown.edu/academics/archaeology/sites/academics-archaeology/files/styles/slide/public/surachi-nuraghe-2014_0.jpg?itok=eblQPa1i" width="861" height="573" alt="" /> 
<div class="overlay">
<h2>Archaeology at Brown University</h2>

  <div class="field-body">
    <p>
	The Joukowsky Institute for Archaeology and the Ancient World promotes the investigation, understanding, and enjoyment of the archaeology and art of the ancient Mediterranean, Egypt, and the Near East.  We work in close collaboration with our colleagues in Brown University's Department of Anthropology whose research is focused on the study of the material remains of the ancient, historic, and modern Americas.
</p>
  </div>
 
</div>
</span>  </div></li>
<li>  
  <div class="views-field views-field-title">        <span class="field-content">
  <img typeof="foaf:Image" src="https://www.brown.edu/academics/archaeology/sites/academics-archaeology/files/styles/slide/public/OtherSideofRome-2016c.jpg?itok=YIFFseue" width="861" height="573" alt="" /> 
<div class="overlay">
<h2>An Interdisciplinary Community</h2>

  <div class="field-body">
    <p>
	The goal of the Institute is to foster an interdisciplinary community of interest in the archaeology of the ancient world, and in the discipline of archaeology more generally.
</p>
  </div>
 
</div>
</span>  </div></li>
<li>  
  <div class="views-field views-field-title">        <span class="field-content">
  <img typeof="foaf:Image" src="https://www.brown.edu/academics/archaeology/sites/academics-archaeology/files/styles/slide/public/styles/slide/public/SLAM2017-KRMR.jpg?itok=8lyic9Hd" width="861" height="573" alt="" /> 
<div class="overlay">
<h2>Our Mandate</h2>

  <div class="field-body">
    <p>
	Our mandate is to promote research, fieldwork, teaching, and public outreach, with the Institute’s associated faculty, students, staff, and facilities serving as a hub for this activity.
</p>
  </div>
 
</div>
</span>  </div></li>
</ul></div>

<div  class="block block-views block-views-fieldwork-featured-project ">
	<div class="width content">
 	 
  	 	   	  <h2 class="title">Featured Project</h2>
 	   	
 	 
 	 

        
  
  
  
        <div class="views-row">
    <article  class="node-project node-promoted node-teaser " about="/academics/archaeology/content/survey-and-landscape-archaeology-montserrat-west-indies" typeof="sioc:Item foaf:Document" role="article">
  
        <h2><a href="/academics/archaeology/content/survey-and-landscape-archaeology-montserrat-west-indies" rel="bookmark">Survey and Landscape Archaeology on Montserrat, West Indies</a></h2>
    <span property="dc:title" content="Survey and Landscape Archaeology on Montserrat, West Indies" class="rdf-meta element-hidden"></span>
  
  <div class="content">
    
  <div class="field-proj-image">
    <a href="/academics/archaeology/content/survey-and-landscape-archaeology-montserrat-west-indies"><img typeof="foaf:Image" src="https://www.brown.edu/academics/archaeology/sites/academics-archaeology/files/styles/large/public/project/media/Montserrat1.JPG?itok=DmNLA-je" width="480" height="360" alt="" /></a>  </div>

  <div class="field-body">
    <p>
	SLAM aims to create a thorough inventory of known and unknown archaeological sites in the northern non-exclusion zone of Montserrat in the West Indies, home to numerous significant prehistoric and historic archaeological remains now under severe threat from volcanic activity and resulting population relocation.
</p>
  </div>
  </div>

  
  </article>

  </div>

  
  
  
  
      <div class="view-footer">
      <div class="view-all"><a href="research-projects/brown-university-fieldwork" class="view-all">View All</a></div>
    </div>

<div  class="block block-views block-views-slide-block ">
	<div class="width content">
 	 
  	 	   	
 	 
 	 

        
  
  
  
      <div  id="flexslider-1" class="flexslider optionset-default">
  <ul class="slides"><li>  
  <div class="views-field views-field-title">        <span class="field-content">
  <img typeof="foaf:Image" src="https://www.brown.edu/academics/archaeology/sites/academics-archaeology/files/styles/slide/public/surachi-nuraghe-2014_0.jpg?itok=eblQPa1i" width="861" height="573" alt="" /> 
<div class="overlay">
<h2>Archaeology at Brown University</h2>

  <div class="field-body">
    <p>
	The Joukowsky Institute for Archaeology and the Ancient World promotes the investigation, understanding, and enjoyment of the archaeology and art of the ancient Mediterranean, Egypt, and the Near East.  We work in close collaboration with our colleagues in Brown University's Department of Anthropology whose research is focused on the study of the material remains of the ancient, historic, and modern Americas.
</p>
  </div>
 
</div>
</span>  </div></li>
<li>  
  <div class="views-field views-field-title">        <span class="field-content">
  <img typeof="foaf:Image" src="https://www.brown.edu/academics/archaeology/sites/academics-archaeology/files/styles/slide/public/OtherSideofRome-2016c.jpg?itok=YIFFseue" width="861" height="573" alt="" /> 
<div class="overlay">
<h2>An Interdisciplinary Community</h2>

  <div class="field-body">
    <p>
	The goal of the Institute is to foster an interdisciplinary community of interest in the archaeology of the ancient world, and in the discipline of archaeology more generally.
</p>
  </div>
 
</div>
</span>  </div></li>
<li>  
  <div class="views-field views-field-title">        <span class="field-content">
  <img typeof="foaf:Image" src="https://www.brown.edu/academics/archaeology/sites/academics-archaeology/files/styles/slide/public/styles/slide/public/SLAM2017-KRMR.jpg?itok=8lyic9Hd" width="861" height="573" alt="" /> 
<div class="overlay">
<h2>Our Mandate</h2>

  <div class="field-body">
    <p>
	Our mandate is to promote research, fieldwork, teaching, and public outreach, with the Institute’s associated faculty, students, staff, and facilities serving as a hub for this activity.
</p>
  </div>
 
</div>
</span>  </div></li>
</ul></div>

</div>

<div  class="block block-views block-views-fieldwork-featured-project ">
	<div class="width content">
 	 
  	 	   	  <h2 class="title">Featured Project</h2>
 	   	
 	 
 	 

        
  
  
  
        <div class="views-row">
    <article  class="node-project node-promoted node-teaser " about="/academics/archaeology/content/survey-and-landscape-archaeology-montserrat-west-indies" typeof="sioc:Item foaf:Document" role="article">
  
        <h2><a href="/academics/archaeology/content/survey-and-landscape-archaeology-montserrat-west-indies" rel="bookmark">Survey and Landscape Archaeology on Montserrat, West Indies</a></h2>
    <span property="dc:title" content="Survey and Landscape Archaeology on Montserrat, West Indies" class="rdf-meta element-hidden"></span>
  
  <div class="content">
    
  <div class="field-proj-image">
    <a href="/academics/archaeology/content/survey-and-landscape-archaeology-montserrat-west-indies"><img typeof="foaf:Image" src="https://www.brown.edu/academics/archaeology/sites/academics-archaeology/files/styles/large/public/project/media/Montserrat1.JPG?itok=DmNLA-je" width="480" height="360" alt="" /></a>  </div>

  <div class="field-body">
    <p>
	SLAM aims to create a thorough inventory of known and unknown archaeological sites in the northern non-exclusion zone of Montserrat in the West Indies, home to numerous significant prehistoric and historic archaeological remains now under severe threat from volcanic activity and resulting population relocation.
</p>
  </div>
  </div>

  
  </article>

  </div>

    <span property="dc:title" content="Byron Hamann, Irina Podgorny, and Felipe Rojas - Fake New World: Skulls, Fossils, Frauds and the..." class="rdf-meta element-hidden"></span>
  
  <div class="content">
    
  <div class="field-start-end-date">
    <time  property="dc:date" datatype="xsd:dateTime" content="2017-10-25T18:00:00-04:00" datetime="2017-10-25T18:00:00-04:00">Wednesday, October 25, 2017</time>  </div>

  <div class="field-start-end-time">
    <time  datetime="2017-10-25T18:00:00-04:00"><div class="date-display-range"><span class="date-display-start" property="dc:date" datatype="xsd:dateTime" content="2017-10-25T18:00:00-04:00">6:00 pm</span> to <span class="date-display-end" property="dc:date" datatype="xsd:dateTime" content="2017-10-25T19:30:00-04:00">7:30 pm</span></div></time>  </div>

<div  class="block block-views block-views-slide-block ">
	<div class="width content">
 	 
  	 	   	
 	 
 	 

        
  
  
  
      <div  id="flexslider-1" class="flexslider optionset-default">
  <ul class="slides"><li>  
  <div class="views-field views-field-title">        <span class="field-content">
  <img typeof="foaf:Image" src="https://www.brown.edu/academics/archaeology/sites/academics-archaeology/files/styles/slide/public/surachi-nuraghe-2014_0.jpg?itok=eblQPa1i" width="861" height="573" alt="" /> 
<div class="overlay">
<h2>Archaeology at Brown University</h2>

  <div class="field-body">
    <p>
	The Joukowsky Institute for Archaeology and the Ancient World promotes the investigation, understanding, and enjoyment of the archaeology and art of the ancient Mediterranean, Egypt, and the Near East.  We work in close collaboration with our colleagues in Brown University's Department of Anthropology whose research is focused on the study of the material remains of the ancient, historic, and modern Americas.
</p>
  </div>
 
</div>
</span>  </div></li>
<li>  
  <div class="views-field views-field-title">        <span class="field-content">
  <img typeof="foaf:Image" src="https://www.brown.edu/academics/archaeology/sites/academics-archaeology/files/styles/slide/public/OtherSideofRome-2016c.jpg?itok=YIFFseue" width="861" height="573" alt="" /> 
<div class="overlay">
<h2>An Interdisciplinary Community</h2>

  <div class="field-body">
    <p>
	The goal of the Institute is to foster an interdisciplinary community of interest in the archaeology of the ancient world, and in the discipline of archaeology more generally.
</p>
  </div>
 
</div>
</span>  </div></li>
<li>  
  <div class="views-field views-field-title">        <span class="field-content">
  <img typeof="foaf:Image" src="https://www.brown.edu/academics/archaeology/sites/academics-archaeology/files/styles/slide/public/styles/slide/public/SLAM2017-KRMR.jpg?itok=8lyic9Hd" width="861" height="573" alt="" /> 
<div class="overlay">
<h2>Our Mandate</h2>

  <div class="field-body">
    <p>
	Our mandate is to promote research, fieldwork, teaching, and public outreach, with the Institute’s associated faculty, students, staff, and facilities serving as a hub for this activity.
</p>
  </div>
 
</div>
</span>  </div></li>
</ul></div>

</div>

<div  class="block block-views block-views-fieldwork-featured-project ">
	<div class="width content">
 	 
  	 	   	  <h2 class="title">Featured Project</h2>
 	   	
 	 
 	 

        
  
  
  
        <div class="views-row">
    <article  class="node-project node-promoted node-teaser " about="/academics/archaeology/content/survey-and-landscape-archaeology-montserrat-west-indies" typeof="sioc:Item foaf:Document" role="article">
  
        <h2><a href="/academics/archaeology/content/survey-and-landscape-archaeology-montserrat-west-indies" rel="bookmark">Survey and Landscape Archaeology on Montserrat, West Indies</a></h2>
    <span property="dc:title" content="Survey and Landscape Archaeology on Montserrat, West Indies" class="rdf-meta element-hidden"></span>
  
  <div class="content">
    
  <div class="field-proj-image">
    <a href="/academics/archaeology/content/survey-and-landscape-archaeology-montserrat-west-indies"><img typeof="foaf:Image" src="https://www.brown.edu/academics/archaeology/sites/academics-archaeology/files/styles/large/public/project/media/Montserrat1.JPG?itok=DmNLA-je" width="480" height="360" alt="" /></a>  </div>

  <div class="field-body">
    <p>
	SLAM aims to create a thorough inventory of known and unknown archaeological sites in the northern non-exclusion zone of Montserrat in the West Indies, home to numerous significant prehistoric and historic archaeological remains now under severe threat from volcanic activity and resulting population relocation.
</p>
  </div>
  </div>

  
  </article>

  </div>

      <div  id="flexslider-1" class="flexslider optionset-default">
  <ul class="slides"><li>  
  <div class="views-field views-field-title">        <span class="field-content">
  <img typeof="foaf:Image" src="https://www.brown.edu/academics/archaeology/sites/academics-archaeology/files/styles/slide/public/surachi-nuraghe-2014_0.jpg?itok=eblQPa1i" width="861" height="573" alt="" /> 
<div class="overlay">
<h2>Archaeology at Brown University</h2>

  <div class="field-body">
    <p>
	The Joukowsky Institute for Archaeology and the Ancient World promotes the investigation, understanding, and enjoyment of the archaeology and art of the ancient Mediterranean, Egypt, and the Near East.  We work in close collaboration with our colleagues in Brown University's Department of Anthropology whose research is focused on the study of the material remains of the ancient, historic, and modern Americas.
</p>
  </div>
 
</div>
</span>  </div></li>
<li>  
  <div class="views-field views-field-title">        <span class="field-content">
  <img typeof="foaf:Image" src="https://www.brown.edu/academics/archaeology/sites/academics-archaeology/files/styles/slide/public/OtherSideofRome-2016c.jpg?itok=YIFFseue" width="861" height="573" alt="" /> 
<div class="overlay">
<h2>An Interdisciplinary Community</h2>

  <div class="field-body">
    <p>
	The goal of the Institute is to foster an interdisciplinary community of interest in the archaeology of the ancient world, and in the discipline of archaeology more generally.
</p>
  </div>
 
</div>
</span>  </div></li>
<li>  
  <div class="views-field views-field-title">        <span class="field-content">
  <img typeof="foaf:Image" src="https://www.brown.edu/academics/archaeology/sites/academics-archaeology/files/styles/slide/public/styles/slide/public/SLAM2017-KRMR.jpg?itok=8lyic9Hd" width="861" height="573" alt="" /> 
<div class="overlay">
<h2>Our Mandate</h2>

  <div class="field-body">
    <p>
	Our mandate is to promote research, fieldwork, teaching, and public outreach, with the Institute’s associated faculty, students, staff, and facilities serving as a hub for this activity.
</p>
  </div>
 
</div>
</span>  </div></li>
</ul></div>

  
  
  
  
  
  

 	 	</div>
</div>
  
          </div>

<div  class="block block-views block-views-fieldwork-featured-project ">
	<div class="width content">
 	 
  	 	   	  <h2 class="title">Featured Project</h2>
 	   	
 	 
 	 

        
  
  
  
        <div class="views-row">
    <article  class="node-project node-promoted node-teaser " about="/academics/archaeology/content/survey-and-landscape-archaeology-montserrat-west-indies" typeof="sioc:Item foaf:Document" role="article">
  
        <h2><a href="/academics/archaeology/content/survey-and-landscape-archaeology-montserrat-west-indies" rel="bookmark">Survey and Landscape Archaeology on Montserrat, West Indies</a></h2>
    <span property="dc:title" content="Survey and Landscape Archaeology on Montserrat, West Indies" class="rdf-meta element-hidden"></span>
  
  <div class="content">
    
  <div class="field-proj-image">
    <a href="/academics/archaeology/content/survey-and-landscape-archaeology-montserrat-west-indies"><img typeof="foaf:Image" src="https://www.brown.edu/academics/archaeology/sites/academics-archaeology/files/styles/large/public/project/media/Montserrat1.JPG?itok=DmNLA-je" width="480" height="360" alt="" /></a>  </div>

  <div class="field-body">
    <p>
	SLAM aims to create a thorough inventory of known and unknown archaeological sites in the northern non-exclusion zone of Montserrat in the West Indies, home to numerous significant prehistoric and historic archaeological remains now under severe threat from volcanic activity and resulting population relocation.
</p>
  </div>
  </div>

  
  </article>

  </div>
